<div id="review_997023774" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/997023774" />
    <a title="Andy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6871962-andy"><img alt="Andy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1563915840p2/6871962.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/997023774?book_show_action=true">Jul 15, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Andy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Andy" href="/user/show/6871962-andy">Andy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer997023774" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9114787567081697806">I either loved or hated each book in this series--I've never had that happen to me before. Book one didn't thrill me, book two was amazing, book three was solid and then I got to book four and was like...<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1408930109ra/10912855.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>Why? Because I realized that apart from Gaelen and Mellandra, I HATED everyone in this series! I actually found myself hoping the Mages would win because all of the good characters are so effing annoying. Let's start with Ellysetta. <br/><br/>Ellie is weak...she's supposed to be this mighty character of l</span>
  <span id="freeText9114787567081697806" style="display:none">I either loved or hated each book in this series--I've never had that happen to me before. Book one didn't thrill me, book two was amazing, book three was solid and then I got to book four and was like...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1408930109ra/10912855.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Why? Because I realized that apart from Gaelen and Mellandra, I HATED everyone in this series! I actually found myself hoping the Mages would win because all of the good characters are so effing annoying. Let's start with Ellysetta. <br><br>Ellie is weak...she's supposed to be this mighty character of light and hope with incredible powers and in some respects she is. BUT whenever something goes wrong, she becomes a sobbing, useless, angsty mess who can't stop blaming herself for EVERY LITTLE THING!! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1410315535ra/11090984.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I cannot stand characters like this. They come across as really self-centred to me because they lay claim to every choice and action made by other characters. They only see the world through the filter of how everything connects to them and everything must, therefore, be their fault. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1410315535ra/11090985.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Why should Ellysetta be taking responsibility for the actions of say Adrial when things don't go well with his truemate? He has his own agency and makes his own life choices so I find her guilt over the whole thing to be really aggravating. All it does is give her more cause to doubt herself, which prevents her from bonding to Rain and causes her to be stuck in an unending loop of guilt. The whole book, I was itching to reach into the story and slap her. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1410315535ra/11090986.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Rain and the other powers in the Tarien Soul universe are equally useless. They've had a thousand years to develop new weapons and technologies just on the off chance that Eld rises again. And do they? Do they? No. They continue to fight as they always have and can't manage to think outside the box. <br><br>Because of this, the Mages constantly outmaneuver them and the Fey allies consistently find themselves up shit creek. I wanted the Mages to win because they tried so hard and they strategized for so long and I could tell that they really wanted it. Whereas, the Fey relied on a path that would have ultimately lead to their total destruction if not for Ellie's sudden onslaught of devastating power. <br><br>What a cop out. <br><br><br>More in my review of Book Five...<br></span>
  <a data-text-id="9114787567081697806" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_50184850" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/50184850" />
    <a title="Heather" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2152770-heather"><img alt="Heather" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1329948532p2/2152770.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/50184850?book_show_action=true">Mar 23, 2009</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Heather" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Heather" href="/user/show/2152770-heather">Heather</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2152770-heather?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2152770-heather?shelf=tairen-soul-series">tairen-soul-series</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer50184850" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12821995494075111937">This is book 4 in the Tairen Soul series, and it really does need to be read in order, as each book builds upon the last. If you pick this book up and read it without reading the previous one you are going to be missing so much.<br/><br/>I LOVE this series, but I didn't feel that this book really moved the story forward much. It mainly covers the coming war between the Eld, and the Fey and their allies, and how everyone is preparing for it. It seemed to drag a little, and by the end I was getting sick of </span>
  <span id="freeText12821995494075111937" style="display:none">This is book 4 in the Tairen Soul series, and it really does need to be read in order, as each book builds upon the last. If you pick this book up and read it without reading the previous one you are going to be missing so much.<br /><br />I LOVE this series, but I didn't feel that this book really moved the story forward much. It mainly covers the coming war between the Eld, and the Fey and their allies, and how everyone is preparing for it. It seemed to drag a little, and by the end I was getting sick of listening to Ellie whine about not being good enough and still worrying that she couldn't control the "darkness" within her. However, that's really just a minor complaint, this is probably my least favorite book of the series, but still worthy of a 5 star rating! I still loved the book and the writing, world building and characters are so rich it's a wonderful epic fantasy about the triumph of good and love.<br /><br />The book is a page turner as it switches between a few different story lines. Rain and Ellie are outcasts from the Fading Lands but still working to defeat Eld, they are also trying to complete their truemate bond. Ellie's family is caught in the war as they are ushered to safety, there is distrust among the Celerian leadership, there is unrest in the Fey leadership; there's so much happening it's impossible to put the book down.<br /><br />This book/series has everything you could ask for; romance, suspense, action, and adventure all wrapped up in superb writing. The secondary characters and story lines are just as rich and developed as the main story. None of the characters are perfect, they are all struggling with their own "demons" (some literally) and insecurities, but it's these flaws that make them so loveable and interesting too read about. It's the attention to the details that really draw you into the story.<br /><br />I can NOT wait for Crown of Crystal Flame to find out how this unforgettable story ends!</span>
  <a data-text-id="12821995494075111937" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText16537418978105935845" style="display:none">I love this series, seriously.<br /><br />But this book was a little frustrating for me. The biggest frustration was that it seemed like Rain and Ellie's problems are a little drawn out. Rain has began the Sheitan's madness because of Ellie's inablity to complete their bond. <span id="freeTextContainer15410341989033480098">just tear my heart out and roast it on a spit. so so so good. wilson, you know how to write an ending! and Ellie are my girl. I can take or leave rain, but Ellie's story i can't get enough of. every book she gets stronger, braver, even though she faces stupid evil and has to learn things about herself no one would ever want to know. but what really makes this book are the supporting characters, Shan and elfeya, Dorian and annoura, and adrial and talisa, wow! however, there was not enough steli, </span>
  <span id="freeText15410341989033480098" style="display:none">just tear my heart out and roast it on a spit. so so so good. wilson, you know how to write an ending! and Ellie are my girl. I can take or leave rain, but Ellie's story i can't get enough of. every book she gets stronger, braver, even though she faces stupid evil and has to learn things about herself no one would ever want to know. but what really makes this book are the supporting characters, Shan and elfeya, Dorian and annoura, and adrial and talisa, wow! however, there was not enough steli, bel, or lillis if you ask me. I don't know if my poor little heart can handle it, but bring on book five!</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('F6jlb2i/fJuwl1HR/L/lDmT9TS+UNVgmZOrCybTttKqg+KKmq4uXqZjKRbfc9GVmEp3D3K8pZ/GvYYtYwaYn3Q==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('l2PoJVs9Lw7k1oud1x9pXzxQ+5snCSU6EMBbG7mDjTwgM6/smAnEPMyLn/v3VOk3SjB1aBwVGu3bSxKKzMgeSw==')})
  }

  <span id="freeText10159106914835317147" style="display:none">C.L. Wilsons unique blend of pulse-pounding action, sweeping epic fantasy, and passionate romance has made her books a favorite read for romance and fantasy readers alike. Praised for exceptional worldbuilding and lyric prose, her critically acclaimed novels have regularly appeared on bestseller lists including the USA Today, the New York Times, and Publishers Weekly.<br /><br />C.Ls novels have won numerous industry and reader-selected awards including, LifetimeTV.coms Best Paranormal debut of 2007, the Gayle Wilson Award of Excellence, two National Readers Choice awards, the Colorado Award of Excellence, and the Holt Medallion. Ms. Wilson is the honored recipient of the PEARL award from Paranormal Romance as the best new author of 2007, and winner of the 2009 PEARL award for best Romantic Fantasy novel. <br /><br />When not torturing her characters mercilessly, C.L. enjoys relaxing with her family in sunny Florida and daydreaming of a world where people exercise in their sleep and chocolate chip cookie dough ice cream is a fat burning food.<br />"</span>
